if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json') != '84403b8d1ff5ef9819022c69d6f1ad7f3550ddc4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json') !== '84403b8d1ff5ef9819022c69d6f1ad7f3550ddc4') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json') !== '516f80692587c768f75a440b504cc90f39d5c509') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json') !== '84403b8d1ff5ef9819022c69d6f1ad7f3550ddc4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/100_whois/whois/json_schema.json');
		}
	}
}
